[35m│[0m  [92m- For addition: "add(value1, value2)" [0m                                                                                                                      [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- For subtraction: "subtract(value1, value2)" (value1 - value2)[0m                                                                                             [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- For multiplication: "multiply(value1, value2)"[0m                                                                                                            [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92m- For division: "divide(value1, value2)" (value1 / value2)[0m                                                                                                  [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m                                                                                                                                                              [35m│[0m
[35m│[0m  [92mCRITICAL - CONTEXT TRACKING:[0m                                                                                                                                [35m│[0m

[35m│[0m  [92m- For "what is that less 1?" → subtract(previous_result, 1)[0m                                                                                                 [35m│[0m
